<script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
	var CmChannelID = document.cookie.match(/CmChannelID=([^;]+)/i)
	var CmChannel  = (CmChannelID && CmChannelID[1] )? CmChannelID[1].toLowerCase():'';
	var u = navigator.userAgent;
	var browserDetect =  {         
		mobile: !!u.match(/AppleWebKit.*Mobile.*/), //是否为移动终端
		ios: !!u.match(/\(i[^;]+;( U;)? CPU.+Mac OS X/), //ios系统
		android: u.indexOf('Android') > -1 || u.indexOf('Linux') > -1, //android终端或系统
		wp:u.indexOf('IEMobile') > -1,//Windows Phone系统
		iPhone: u.indexOf('iPhone') > -1 , //是否为iPhone或者QQHD浏览器
		Safari:u.indexOf("Safari") > -1,//判断是否Safari浏览器
		iPad: u.indexOf('iPad') > -1, //是否iPad
		webApp: u.indexOf('Safari') > -1 //是否web应该程序，没有头部与底部
	};
	if ( CmChannel !='pc' && CmChannel != 'pad' && browserDetect.mobile && !browserDetect.iPad ){
		var urlmap = {
			touch : "http://touch.10086.cn/mall_200_663.html",
			wap : 'http://wap.10086.cn/'
		}
		if(CmChannel == 'wap' && urlmap.wap){
			location.href=urlmap.wap;
		}else{
			location.href=urlmap.touch;
		}
	} 

})();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
(function(){
	function screenResize () {
		var ScreenWidth = window.screen.width;
		var client_Width = document.body.clientWidth;
		var html_ele = document.getElementsByTagName("html");
		var sw = '';
		if (ScreenWidth < 1200 || client_Width < 1200) {
			sw = 'w1k';
		}
		html_ele[0].className=sw;
		if(window.$ && $.pub){
			$.pub('wkresize',sw);
		}
	}
	screenResize();

	if (window.addEventListener) {                    //所有主流浏览器，除了 IE 8 及更早 IE版本
	    var tid = null;
		window.addEventListener('onorientationchange' in window ? 'orientationchange' : 'resize', function () {
		    clearTimeout(tid);
		    tid = setTimeout(screenResize, 300);
		}, false);
	} else if (window.attachEvent) {                  // IE 8 及更早 IE 版本
	   	var tid = null;
		window.attachEvent('onorientationchange' in window ? 'onorientationchange' : 'onresize', function () {
		    clearTimeout(tid);
		    tid = setTimeout(screenResize, 300);
		});
	}
})();
</script>

var _options = null
var _spritebox = null;
function __mini_login(event,options){
	_options = options;
	var miniframe = $('#login_box').html();
	if(miniframe){
		_spritebox  = $('#jquery-interactive-box2').hide();
		$('#jquery-interactive-mask').hide();
		var $box = $.alert(miniframe,{
			onLoad:function($box){
				$box.find('.interactive-content').css({
					'background-color':'#ECECEC'
				});
			},
			onClose:function(){
				$.pub('login_mini_cancel');
				_options = null;
				_spritebox = null;
				$.UI.hide();
			},
			liveTime:null,
			noCloser:false
		});
		return false;
	}else{
		return true;
	}
}	
function __mini_login_msg(event , r){
	if(window.initUser){
		window.initUser(r);
	}
	$.UI.hide('alert');
	if(r.code == 0){
		if(_options && typeof _options == 'object' )$.ajax(_options);
		_options = null;
		if(_spritebox && _spritebox.length){
			$('#jquery-interactive-mask').show();
			_spritebox.show();
		}
		_spritebox = null;
	}else {
		$.UI.hide();
	}
}

			;
			$(function() {
			  $.getJSON('/ajax/cartshop/amount.json', function(r) {
			  		if (r.code) {
			  			$.alert(r.msg);
			  		} else{	
			  			$('.cart .red').text(r.data.num);
			  			$('#returntop .cart-quan em').text(r.data.num);
						$('.have_goods .btm .cartcount b').text(r.data.num);
			  		};
			  });
				$
				.sub('mouseover_cart1_count',__cart1_count)
				.sub('msg_cart',__cart1_show,false)
				;
				var list_lock = true;

					function __cart1_count(){
						if(list_lock){
							$.getJSON('/ajax/cartshop/list.json',function(r){
								if(r.code){
									$.alert(r.msg);
								}else {
									$.pub('msg_cart', r.data);
								}
							});
						}
						list_lock = false;
					}


				function __cart1_show(event,r){
					var  cartdata = r;
					var $cart_list =[];
					var $cartcount =null;
					if (cartdata && cartdata.cartcount) {
						var  total = 0 ,count = 0;
						$('.dorpdown-layer .cart_list .mCSB_container').html(cartdata.content);
						$('.have_goods .cartcount b,.rightMenu .cart .red,.rightfloatbox .cart-quan em').html(cartdata.cartcount);
						$cart_list = $('.rightMenu .cart_list').find('li');
						if ($cart_list.length > 5) {
							$('.cart_list').addClass('height268');
						}else{
							$('.cart_list').removeClass('height268');
						};
						$($cart_list).each(function () {
							var $t = $(this);
							total +=parseInt($t.attr('num'))*parseInt($t.attr('price')*100)||0;
							//count +=parseInt($t.attr('num'))||0;
						});
						$('.have_goods .btm .red b').text((total/100).toFixed(2));
						//$('.have_goods .btm .cartcount b').text(count);
						$cartcount = $('.cart_list ul').attr('cartcount');
						if($cart_list.length == 0 && $cartcount){
							$('.dorpdown-layer .loadingBlock').hide();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods_p').hide();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .abate').show();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods').show();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods').hide();
						}else{
							$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods').hide();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .loadingBlock').hide();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods').show();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .cart_goodslist').show();
							$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods .btm').show();
						}
					}else{
						$('.have_goods .cartcount b,.rightMenu .cart .red,.rightfloatbox .cart-quan em').html('0');
						$('.dorpdown-layer .loadingBlock').hide();
						$('.dorpdown-layer .abate').hide();
						$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods_p').show();
						$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods').show();
						$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods').hide();
					};

				}

			  var timer = null;
			  $('.cart').hover(function() {
			  	var is_cart = '';
			  	if (is_cart) return false;
			  	clearTimeout(timer);
			  	$(".rightMenu .dorpdown-layer").show();
				  //__hover_get_cart();

			  }, function() {

					list_lock = true;

			  });
			  $('.dorpdown-layer').hover(function() {
				  list_lock = false;
			  	clearTimeout(timer);
				  $('.cart').addClass('current');
			  	$(this).show();
			  }, function() {
				  timer = setTimeout(function () {
					  list_lock = true;
				  	$('.cart').removeClass('current');

			  	},100);

			  $

			  ;
			  function __cartlist_delete() {
					var $t = $(this);
					var cartcount = $t.closest('ul').attr('cartcount');
					$.getJSON('/ajax/cartshop/delete.json',{selected: $t.closest('li').attr('cartid')},function(r){
						if (r.code) {
							$.alert(r.msg);
						} else{
							$t.closest('li').remove();
							$cart_list = $('.rightMenu .cart_list').find('li');
							if ($cart_list.length > 5) {
								$('.cart_list').addClass('height268');
							}else{
								$('.cart_list').removeClass('height268');
							};
							$.pub('cartlist_del');
						};
					});
				}

				function cartlist_del () {
					var c_num = $('.cart .red').text();
					$('.have_goods .cartcount b,.rightMenu .cart .red,.rightfloatbox .cart-quan em').text(parseInt(c_num-1));
			  		$('#returntop .cart-quan em').text(parseInt(c_num-1));
			  		var total = 0;
			  		var $cart_list = $('.rightMenu .cart_list').find('li');
					$($cart_list).each(function () {
						var $t = $(this);
						total +=parseInt($t.attr('num'))*parseInt($t.attr('price')*100)||0;
					});
					$('.have_goods .btm .red b').text((total/100).toFixed(2));
			  		if (c_num && c_num-1 != 0) {
			  			$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods').hide();
                		$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods').show();
			  		} else{
			  			$('.dorpdown-layer .nogoods').show();
                		$('.dorpdown-layer .have_goods').hide();
			  		};
				}
			});
			
			
				
                    $(document).ready(function(){
                        var timers = null;

                        $(".cmccclient").hover(function() {
                            clearTimeout(timers);
                            var cmcc_left_1 = $('.cmccclient').position().left+2;
                            $('.ewm').css('left', cmcc_left_1);
                            $('.ewm').show();
                        }, function() {
                            timers = setTimeout(function () {
                                $('.ewm').hide();
                            },100);
                        });
                        $('.ewm').hover(function() {
                        	var cmcc_left_2 = $('.cmccclient').position().left+2;
                            clearTimeout(timers);
                            $('.cmccclient').addClass('cmccclienthover');
                            $(this).css('left', cmcc_left_2);
                            $(this).show();
                        }, function() {
                            var $t = $(this);
                            timers = setTimeout(function(){
                                $('.cmccclient').removeClass('cmccclienthover');
                                $t.hide();
                            },100);
                        });
                    });
				
				
	
	window.initUser = function(r){
		if(r.code == 0){
			window.loginUser = r.data;
			var nickname = r.data.nick_name || r.data.user_name
			var tmpnick = nickname.split('@')[0];
            var noread = (r.data.msg_remind ||{}).noread || 0;
			if(tmpnick.length>=15) tmpnick = tmpnick.substr(0,14) +"...";
			var tmpstr =
                    '<span class="floatleft marginRight10" title="' + nickname + '">' + tmpnick + '</span>'+ 
                    '<span class="floatleft noticearea" >'+
                    ' <a href="http://shop.10086.cn/i/?f=mynews"  target="_blank" class="red floatleft">消息 ' + noread + '</a> </span>'+ 
                    '<a class="red bold" href="javascript:void(logout())" title="退出">[退 出]</a><em>|</em>';
			document.getElementById('userinfo').innerHTML = tmpstr;
			if ($.pub){
				$.pub('login_success' ,r.data);
			}
		}else if (r.code == 3 ){
			$('#ssocheckframe').attr('src' ,r.data);
		}else{
			$('.btnOnestepbuy').hide();
			var $osb = $('.btnOnestepbuy').attr('osb');
			var osbmaskShow = $.cookie("osbmaskShow");
			if($osb&&!osbmaskShow){
				$('.onestepbuymask').show();
				$.cookie("osbmaskShow","true",{expires : 1000});
			}

		}
	}
	var userParam = {
		'province_id' : '200',
		'city_id' : '663'
	}	
			userParam.update = 1;
		$.getJSON('/ajax/user/userinfo.json',userParam,initUser);

	$(function(){
		$
		.sub('click_show_areabar',__show_areabar)
		.sub('click_show_city',__show_city)
		.sub('click_city_choose',__gotocity)
		;

		//清除浮层
		function __clear_areabar(){
			$('#header').find('.area ul').hide();
		}
		//展开浮层
		function __show_areabar(){
			__clear_areabar();
			var $this = $(this);
			$this.next().show();
			return false;
		}
		function __gotocity(loc){
			if(typeof loc != "string"){
				loc = $(this).attr('location');
			}
			var locarray = loc.split('_');
			var pid = locarray[0],cid = locarray[1];
			var url = location.href ;
			if(url.indexOf('/list/') > 0){
				url = url.replace(/_\d{3}_\d{3,4}/i,"_"+loc);
				setTimeout(function(){
					location.href=url;
				});
			}else{
				setTimeout(function(){
					location.href="/mall_{loc}.html".replace("{loc}",loc);
				});
			}
		}
		function getCityByProvince(province_id){
			if ( !window.allcity[province_id] ){
				$.ajax({
					async : false,
					url : "/ajax/region/singleregion.json",
					data:{province_id:province_id},
					success:function(r){
						if(r.code){
							$.alert(r.msg)
						}else{
							window.allcity[province_id] = r.data || [];
						}
					},
					dataType:'json'
				});
			}
			return window.allcity[province_id];
		}
		var $province = $('#header .province'),
			$city = $('#header .city'),
			current_province_id = $province.find('span').attr('province_id'),
			city_id = '663',
			reg = new RegExp('<!--|-->','g') ,
			template = new Formater($('.header_area_template').html().replace(reg,'')||'<li><a href="#" target="_blank">{city_name}</a></li>'),
			city_name = '揭阳'
			;
		//点击省下拉项展开市浮层
		function __show_city(){
			var $this = $(this),
				province_id = $this.attr('province_id'),
				tmp=''
			;
			if( $this.attr('iscity')) {
				__gotocity(province_id+"_"+province_id);
				return false;
			}
			var data=getCityByProvince(province_id);
			$city.find('span').text('请选择');
			//var cityAreaWidth = (data.length < 4) ? 40*(data.length + 1) + 5 : 245;//根据市的个数，判断外框宽度
			$.each(data,function(inx,item){
				tmp+=template.exec(item);
			});
			__clear_areabar();
			$this.closest('ul').prev().attr('province_id',$this.attr('province_id')).text($this.text());
			$city.find('ul').html(tmp).show();
			return false;	
		}

		//点击其他dom收起浮层
		$(document).bind('click.area',function(e){
			if($(e.target).closest('.area').length == 0){
				__clear_areabar();
			}

		});

	})
	;

$(function() {
	//banner部分
	var $banner = $('#focus'),
		$bannerLi = $banner.find('li'),
		$liWidth = $bannerLi.eq(0).width(),
		$btnsHtml = '<p class="btns">',
		bannerCurrent = 0,
		timeBanner = 0;
	//计算ul宽度
	//$banner.find('ul').width($liWidth*$bannerLi.length);
	$bannerLi.each(function(i,item){
		if(i == 0){
			$btnsHtml += '<span class="current">1</span>';
		}else{
			$btnsHtml += '<span>' + (i+1) + '</span>';
		}
	});
	$btnsHtml += '</p>';
	$banner.append($btnsHtml);
	$banner.find('.btns span').click(function(){
		var $this = $(this);
		clickIndex = $banner.find('.btns span').index($this);
		if(clickIndex != bannerCurrent){
			$bannerLi.eq(bannerCurrent).fadeOut(800);
			$bannerLi.eq(clickIndex).fadeIn(800);
			bannerCurrent = clickIndex;
			$this.addClass('current').siblings('span').removeClass('current');
		}
	});
	
	function bannerNext(){
		clearTimeout(timeBanner);
		if(bannerCurrent >= $bannerLi.length-1){
			$banner.find('.btns span').eq(0).triggerHandler('click');
		}else{
			$banner.find('.btns span').eq(bannerCurrent +1).triggerHandler('click');
		}
		timeBanner = setTimeout(bannerNext,3000);
	}
	timeBanner = setTimeout(bannerNext,6000);
	$banner.hover(function(){
		clearTimeout(timeBanner);
	},function(){
		timeBanner = setTimeout(bannerNext,3000);
	});

	
});




$(function() {
	

	//banner下方图片
	var $slideBox = $('#bannerSlide'),
		$slideLi = $slideBox.find('li'),
		liWidth = $slideLi.eq(0).outerWidth(),
		timeSlide = 0;
	$slideBox.find('ul').width($slideLi.length*liWidth);
	if($slideLi.length >3){
		$slideBox.find('.turn_left, .turn_right').show();
	}
	$slideBox.find('.turn_left, .turn_right').click(function(){
		if(!$slideBox.find('ul').is(':animated') && $slideLi.length >3){
			var $this = $(this);
			var clickIndex = ($this.hasClass('turn_left'))?-1:1;
			if(clickIndex == -1){
				$slideBox.find('ul').css('left',-liWidth).find('li:last').prependTo($slideBox.find('ul')).end().end().animate({
					'left':0
				});
			}else if(clickIndex == 1){
				$slideBox.find('ul').animate({
					'left':-liWidth
				},function(){
					$slideBox.find('li:first').appendTo($slideBox.find('ul'));
					$slideBox.find('ul').css('left',0);
				});
			}
		}
	});
	function autoSlide(){
		clearTimeout(timeSlide);
		$slideBox.find('.turn_right').triggerHandler('click');
		timeSlide = setTimeout(autoSlide,3000);
	}
	timeSlide = setTimeout(autoSlide,4000);
	$slideBox.hover(function(){
		$slideBox.find('.turn_left').stop().animate({
			left:0
		});
		$slideBox.find('.turn_right').stop().animate({
			right:0
		});
		clearTimeout(timeSlide);
	},function(){
		$slideBox.find('.turn_left').stop().animate({
			left:'-28px'
		});
		$slideBox.find('.turn_right').stop().animate({
			right:'-28px'
		});
		timeSlide = setTimeout(autoSlide,3000);
	});
});

$(function(){
	//号码左右滚动
	var $numSlideBox = $('.modGoods .numList');
	$numSlideBox.find('.turnLeft, .turnRight').click(function(){
		var $this = $(this);
		if($this.hasClass('turnLeft')){
			$numSlideBox.find('li:last').prependTo($numSlideBox.find('ul'));
		}else{
			$numSlideBox.find('li:first').appendTo($numSlideBox.find('ul'));
		}
	});
	//号码组换一组操作
	var p = 0;
	var param = {
			rows:11,
			province_id:"200",
			city_id:"663"
		};
	var number_total = 0;
	var template = new Formater($('#numberTemplate').html());
	function getNextNums(){
		$.getJSON('/ajax/number/get4flist.json',param,function(r){
			if(r.code){
				$.alert(r.msg);
			}else{
				number_total = r.data.goods_total;
				p = Math.floor(Math.random()*Math.ceil(number_total/6) + 1);
				param.p = p;
				var r_html = '';
				$(r.data.goods_list).each(function(i,item){
					item.index=i;
					item.numstr = item.number_name.substring(0,3) + ' <em>' + item.number_name.substring(3,7) + '</em> ' + item.number_name.substring(7,11);
					r_html +=template.exec(item);
				});
				$('#numListArea').html(r_html);
			}
		});
	}
	getNextNums();
	$('.numRight .btnBlue').click(function(){
		getNextNums();
	});
	$('.numSearch ul li').click(function(){
		$('.numSearch .title p').text($(this).text());
		$(this).addClass('current').siblings().removeClass('current');
	});
	var $numInputs =  $('.numSearch input');
	$numInputs.keyup(function(){
		if(this.value.length == 1){
			var $t= $(this);
			$.dcstracker({
				category:'Home',
				action:'NUMBER',
				event:$t.attr('dcs_id')
			});
			$t.next().focus();
		}
	});
	$('#numBtn').click(function(){
		var $t=$(this) , str = $.trim($('.numSearch .title p').text()) , isjump=true;
		$numInputs.each(function(){
			//号码只准写数字
			var re = new RegExp('^[0-9]+$|^$','g');
			if(!re.test($.trim($(this).val()))){
				$(this).notice("请输入数字").focus();
				isjump=false;
				return false
			}
			str += $.trim($(this).val())|| '*';
		});
		$.dcstracker({
			category:'Home',
			action:'NUMBER',
			event:$t.attr('dcs_id')
		});
		if(isjump){
			setTimeout(function(){
			location.href="/list/134_200_663_0_0_0_0.html?key="+str;
			},500);
		}
	});
	//.numSearch .title 点击其他document下拉框收起
	$(document).bind('click.numselect',function(e){
		if($(e.target).closest('.numSearch .title').length == 0){
			$('.numSearch .title').removeClass('current');
		}
	});

	$
	.sub('click_dcstracker_NUMBER_AD',__dcstracker_numberad)
	.sub('click_dcstracker_numbermenu',__dcstracker_numbermenu)
	.sub('click_dcstracker_numberphone',__dcstracker_numberphone)
	.sub('click_dcstracker_numberhd',__dcstracker_numberhd)
	.sub('click_dcstracker_numbermore',__dcstracker_numbermore)
	;

		var $t= $(this);

			category:'Home',

			event:$t.attr('dcs_id')
		});

;$(function(){
	$
	.sub('click_dcstracker_ACCESSORY_AD',__dcstracker_accessoryad)

	var zhekou,zhekou_cache = {};
	function recharge_zhekou (argument1,argument2) {
		if(argument2){
			zhekou = zhekou_cache[argument2];
		}else if (argument1){
			zhekou = zhekou_cache[argument1];
		}else {
			zhekou = null ;
			zhekou_show();
			return ;
		}
		if(zhekou) {
			zhekou_show();	
			return;
		}

		$.getJSON('/ajax/recharge/recharge.json', {province_id:argument1,phone_num:argument2}, function(r){
			if (r.code) {
				$.alert(r.msg);
			} else{
				if(argument2){
					zhekou_cache[argument2] = r.data;
				}else {
					zhekou_cache[argument1]	 = r.data;
				}
				zhekou=r.data;
				zhekou_show();
			}
		});
	}
	function zhekou_show () {
	 	var jine=$('.con_hfcz input[name=amount]').val();

	 		$('.con_hfcz .zhekou').text(zhekou[jine]);
	 	} else{
	 		$('.con_hfcz .zhekou').text('');
	 	};
	 }

			},300);
		}

	function __index_chongzhi () {
		var $this = $(this);
		flag = $this.closest('.cz').attr('flag');
		$this.closest('.yuan').find('.yuan_show').text($this.text());
		$this.closest('.yuan').find('.yuan_show').attr('traffic', $this.attr('traffic'));
		if (flag == 1) {
			$this.parent().siblings('input[name=amount]').val(parseInt($this.text()));
			mobileNo = $('.con_hfcz').find('input[name="phonenum"]').val();
			amount = $('.con_hfcz').find('input[name="amount"]').val();
		} else if(flag == 2){
			$this.parent().parent().siblings('input[name=amount]').val(parseInt($this.attr('traffic')));
			mobileNo = $('.con_llcz').find('input[name="phonenum"]').val();
			amount = $('.con_llcz').find('input[name="amount"]').val();
		}else{

		};
		var discount = null;
		if(flag == 2 ) {
			var dc = dataMap[$this.attr('traffic')];
			if(dc && dc.discountList && dc.discountList.length){
				discount = dc.discountList[0];
				if(discount){
					discount = (discount.discountCnt == 100)? null : discount.discountCnt;
				}
			}
		}
		if (discount) {
			$this.closest('.cz').find('.discoutsize').text(discount/10);
			$this.closest('dl').next().find('.price_num').text(parseInt($this.attr('pay_num') ) * discount/100);
			$this.closest('.cz').find('.price').css('color', '#ed2668');
			$this.closest('.cz').find('.discount_zhe').show();
		}else{
			$this.closest('.cz').find('.price').css('color', '#666');
			$this.closest('dl').next().find('.price_num').text(parseInt($this.attr('pay_num')));
			$this.closest('.cz').find('.discount_zhe').hide();
		}
		$this.closest('.select_yuan').hide();
		d_show = $this.text();
		p_show = $this.attr('pay_num');
		zhekou_show();
		initUrl();
		
	}

	function initUrl(){

		if (flag && flag == 1) {
			mobileNo = $('.con_hfcz').find('input[name="phonenum"]').val();
			amount = $('.con_hfcz').find('input[name="amount"]').val();
		} else if (flag && flag == 2){
			mobileNo = $('.con_llcz').find('input[name="phonenum_ll"]').val();
			amount = $('.con_llcz').find('input[name="amount"]').val();
		}else{

		};

		var data = {
			mobileNo : mobileNo,
			amount: amount
		}
		if(isNaN(data.mobileNo)){
			delete data.mobileNo;
		}
		$rechargeBtn.attr("href",url+"&"+ $.param(data))
	}
	
	//手机号默认文字
	$('.recharge .number input[name="phonenum"],.recharge .number input[name="phonenum_ll"]').iPrompt({
		refer:'iprompt'
	});
	initUrl();

	function draw(arr,arrs){
		var $area = $('.countdown');
		var $em = $area.find('em') , len = $em.length , data = arr , arr_a = [] ;
		if (len == 8){
			day = ('0'+ arr[0]).slice(-2);
			var daya = day.substring(0,1) , dayb = day.substring(1);
			arr_a.push(daya,dayb);
			$.each(arrs,function(index,item){
				arr_a.push(item);
			});
			data = arr_a;
		}
		$em.each(function(index,item){
		  $(item).text(data[index]);
		});
	}
	window.drawCountdown = draw;
});

$(function(){
	$
	.sub('click_footer_sdc',__footer_sdc)
	.sub('login_success',__userinfo_sdc)
	;
	function __footer_sdc(){
		var $t= $(this);
		$.dcstracker({
			action:'footer_fast_link',
			event:$t.attr('dcs')
		});
	}

	function __userinfo_sdc (){
		if( window.loginUser){
			var user = window.loginUser;
			var dcsdata = {'event':'userinfo'};
			if(user.user_type == '01'){
				dcsdata.mobile = user.user_name;
			}else{
				dcsdata.user_name = user.user_name;
			}
			$.dcstracker(dcsdata);
		}
	}
});

(function(){
	function screenResize () {
		var ScreenWidth = window.screen.width;
		var client_Width = document.body.clientWidth;
		var html_ele = document.getElementsByTagName("html");
		var sw = '';
		if (ScreenWidth < 1200 || client_Width < 1200) {
			sw = 'w1k';
		}
		html_ele[0].className=sw;
		if(window.$ && $.pub){
			$.pub('wkresize',sw);
		}
	}
	screenResize();

	if (window.addEventListener) {                    //所有主流浏览器，除了 IE 8 及更早 IE版本
	    var tid = null;
		window.addEventListener('onorientationchange' in window ? 'orientationchange' : 'resize', function () {
		    clearTimeout(tid);
		    tid = setTimeout(screenResize, 300);
		}, false);
	} else if (window.attachEvent) {                  // IE 8 及更早 IE 版本
	   	var tid = null;
		window.attachEvent('onorientationchange' in window ? 'onorientationchange' : 'onresize', function () {
		    clearTimeout(tid);
		    tid = setTimeout(screenResize, 300);
		});
	}
})();
</script>

			  function __cartlist_delete() {
					var $t = $(this);

					$.getJSON('/ajax/cartshop/delete.json',{selected: $t.closest('li').attr('cartid')},function(r){

				function cartlist_del () {
					var c_num = $('.cart .red').text();
					$('.have_goods .cartcount b,.rightMenu .cart .red,.rightfloatbox .cart-quan em').text(parseInt(c_num-1));

	window.initUser = function(r){
		if(r.code == 0){
			window.loginUser = r.data;

			var tmpnick = nickname.split('@')[0];

                    '<span class="floatleft noticearea" >'+

                    '<a class="red bold" href="javascript:void(logout())" title="退出">[退 出]</a><em>|</em>';
			document.getElementById('userinfo').innerHTML = tmpstr;
			if ($.pub){
				$.pub('login_success' ,r.data);
			}
		}else if (r.code == 3 ){
			$('#ssocheckframe').attr('src' ,r.data);
		}else{
			$('.btnOnestepbuy').hide();
			var $osb = $('.btnOnestepbuy').attr('osb');
			var osbmaskShow = $.cookie("osbmaskShow");
			if($osb&&!osbmaskShow){
				$('.onestepbuymask').show();
				$.cookie("osbmaskShow","true",{expires : 1000});
			}

		}
	}

		//清除浮层
		function __clear_areabar(){
			$('#header').find('.area ul').hide();

		function __show_areabar(){

		function __gotocity(loc){
			if(typeof loc != "string"){
				loc = $(this).attr('location');
			}
			var locarray = loc.split('_');
			var pid = locarray[0],cid = locarray[1];
			var url = location.href ;
			if(url.indexOf('/list/') > 0){
				url = url.replace(/_\d{3}_\d{3,4}/i,"_"+loc);
				setTimeout(function(){
					location.href=url;
				});
			}else{
				setTimeout(function(){
					location.href="/mall_{loc}.html".replace("{loc}",loc);
				});
			}
		}
		function getCityByProvince(province_id){
			if ( !window.allcity[province_id] ){
				$.ajax({
					async : false,
					url : "/ajax/region/singleregion.json",
					data:{province_id:province_id},
					success:function(r){
						if(r.code){
							$.alert(r.msg)
						}else{
							window.allcity[province_id] = r.data || [];
						}
					},
					dataType:'json'
				});
			}
			return window.allcity[province_id];
		}

			$city = $('#header .city'),

			reg = new RegExp('<!--|-->','g') ,
			template = new Formater($('.header_area_template').html().replace(reg,'')||'<li><a href="#" target="_blank">{city_name}</a></li>'),
			city_name = '揭阳'
			;
		//点击省下拉项展开市浮层
		function __show_city(){
			var $this = $(this),
				province_id = $this.attr('province_id'),
				tmp=''
			;
			if( $this.attr('iscity')) {
				__gotocity(province_id+"_"+province_id);
				return false;
			}
			var data=getCityByProvince(province_id);
			$city.find('span').text('请选择');
			//var cityAreaWidth = (data.length < 4) ? 40*(data.length + 1) + 5 : 245;//根据市的个数，判断外框宽度
			$.each(data,function(inx,item){
				tmp+=template.exec(item);
			});
			__clear_areabar();
			$this.closest('ul').prev().attr('province_id',$this.attr('province_id')).text($this.text());
			$city.find('ul').html(tmp).show();
			return false;	
		}

		//点击其他dom收起浮层
		$(document).bind('click.area',function(e){
			if($(e.target).closest('.area').length == 0){
				__clear_areabar();
			}

		});

	})
	;
	
	

;$(function(){
	$(".quan_thead .tag").click(function(){
	  $(".quan_thead .tag").removeClass("current");
	  $(this).addClass("current");
	});
	$(".quan_thead .tag1").click(function(){
		$(".quan_main .con1").show();
		$(".quan_main .con2").hide();

	});
	$(".quan_thead .tag2").click(function(){
		$(".quan_main .con2").show();
		$(".quan_main .con1").hide();

	});

	$
	.sub('click_use_coupon',__use_coupon,true)
	.sub('click_pay_type',__check_coupon_paytype,false)
	;

	$('.ac_use_coupon').attr('checked',false);
	function __use_coupon () {
		var $t = $(this),ticket_no = $t.val(),cart_code=ENVOBJ.cart_code;
		var checked_status = $t.attr('checked');
		$t.attr('checked','checked').closest('li').siblings().find('.ac_use_coupon').attr('checked', false);
		if (checked_status == 'checked') {
			$t.attr('checked', false);
			ticket_no = '';
		} else{
			ticket_no = $t.val();
		};
		$.post('/ajax/coupon/batchdetail.json', {ticket_no:ticket_no,cart_code:cart_code}, function(r) {
			if (r.code && r.code == 16) {
				$.alert(r.msg);
				window.location.href = window.location.href;
			}else if(r.code){
				$.alert(r.msg);
			} else{
				if($("#orderform").length ){
					$('#orderform input[name=ticket_no]').val(ticket_no);
					$('.summary_cart .total_price').text('¥ '+(r.data.sum/100).toFixed(2));
					$('.summary_cart .youhui_price').text('- ¥ '+(r.data.reduce_price/100).toFixed(2));
					$('.summary_cart .real_price, .summary_area .real_price').text('¥ '+(r.data.pay_price/100).toFixed(2));
				}
			};
		}, 'JSON');
		
	}
	function __check_coupon_paytype(){
		var flag = ($(this).attr('pay_type') == "1");
		$('input[name=ticket_no]:checked').click();
		$('input[name=ticket_no]:checked').attr('checked', false);
		$('.quan_main .con1 .ac_use_coupon , #orderform input[name=ticket_no]').prop('disabled' ,!flag);
		if(flag == false){
			$('.quan_thead dd').hide();		
			$('.quan_thead #quantips').show();		
			$('.quan_main').hide();
		}else{
			$('.quan_thead dd').show();		
			$('.quan_thead #quantips').hide();		
			$('.quan_main').show();
		}
	}
	$('.ac_pay_type').eq(0).click();
});

	}

		})

});

                   if (isIE6()) {

                        var sTop = $(window).scrollTop();
                        var h = parseInt(wheight + sTop);
                        $('.lowerIEtips').stop().animate({marginTop:h},1).show();
                   }
                }
            }).scroll();
